  <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div>
<h2 id="user-content-electornic-data-interchange"><a id="user-content-electornic-data-interchange" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#electornic-data-interchange"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Electornic Data Interchange</h2>
<div>
<table>





<thead>
<tr>
<th>version</th>
<th>section</th>
<th>schema</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><p>04.2020</p></td>
<td><p>1.0.0</p></td>
<td><p>X12</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<div>
<p><strong>EDI File Structure</strong></p>
</div>
<div>
<p>Contains a tree-like structure of the EDI file in terms of loops and segments Format ` {:&lt;RepeatCount|&gt;1&gt;&lt;[SegmentName [*MaskNumber], Usage]&gt;[{}]} `</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<h2 id="user-content-open-edi-script"><a id="user-content-open-edi-script" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#open-edi-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Open EDI Script</h2>
<div>
<div>
<p>A Domain Specific Language to enable better mappings of EDI transactions and offer greater extensibility while adhereing to the specifications.</p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-lisp"><pre># <span class="pl-k">if</span> then, end

SegPos = <span class="pl-k">if</span> (Condition|CodeCondition) then Usage|LocalCode|Error end


# <span class="pl-k">if</span>-then, <span class="pl-k">else</span>-end

SegPos = <span class="pl-k">if</span> (Condition|CodeCondition) then Usage|LocalCode|Error <span class="pl-k">else</span> Usage|LocalCode|Error end

# <span class="pl-k">if</span>-then, elseif-then-end
SegPos = <span class="pl-k">if</span> (Condition|CodeCondition) then Usage|LocalCode|Error elseif (Condition) then Usage|LocalCode|Error end</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<h3 id="user-content-defintions"><a id="user-content-defintions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#defintions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Defintions</h3>
<div>
<h4 id="user-content-segpos"><a id="user-content-segpos" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#segpos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>SegPos</h4>
<div>
<p>The segment position we want to modify.
Ordinal values are used.
For example SegPos[1] is the ISA segment.
SegPos[1:2] will be the second element of segment ISA.
SegPos[1:2:1] would be ISA02 composite element 1</p>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<h4 id="user-content-condition"><a id="user-content-condition" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#condition"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Condition</h4>
<div>
<p>A condition that must evaluate to true before the statement in the then clause can execute.
`+SegPos[27] = if (SegPos[26:2] == "18") then Usage[Optional] else Usage[NotUsed] end `</p>
</div>
<div>
<p>[Segment/Element Position]=(Condition):ActionType:(true USAGE):(default USAGE)</p>
</div>
<div>
<p>ActionType is either USAGE or LOCALCODE</p>
</div>
<div>
<p>27=26:2’EQ'18!USAGE!0!1 31=26:2’EQ'18!USAGE!2!0 40=26:2’EQ'18!USAGE!2!1 146=140:1’EQ’R,S!USAGE!2!0 207=26:2’NE'18!USAGE!2!1 321=315:1’EQ’R,S!USAGE!2!0</p>
</div>
<div>
<p>Example</p>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-lisp"><pre>{INTERCHANGE HEADER:1[ISA,M]{FUNCTIONAL GROUP:1[GS,M]{ST ST HEADER LOOP:1[+SE,M]}}{END GS LOOP:1[+GE,M]}}{END ISA LOOP:1[+IEA,M]}}</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div>
<p>Each segment that appears in the structure has an implicit ordinal value beginning with 1.
For example segment ISA has an ordinal value of 1, segment GS has an ordinal value of 2, ST has an ordinal value of 3 and BHT has an ordinal value of 4.
This ordinal value is what uniquely identifies each segment in the structure.</p>
</div>
<hr>
